### Round 5: Monaco Grand Prix
*Date: 1995-05-28*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 9: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1995-07-30*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 12: Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 1995-09-10*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 15: Pacific Grand Prix
*Date: 1995-10-22*

#### Qualifying Results
